<script>document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

  function jumpToRecipe() {
    const el = document.getElementById('recipe');
    if (!el) return;

    // Update the URL hash manually so sharing/back works,
    // but ONLY after reward is granted.
    if (history.pushState) {
      history.pushState(null, '', '#recipe');
    } else {
      // fallback for ancient browsers
      window.location.hash = '#recipe';
    }

    el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }

  function showRewardedThenMaybeJump() {
    // Fallback: if ezRewardedAds isn't available, just jump right now
    if (
      !window.ezRewardedAds ||
      typeof window.ezRewardedAds.requestWithOverlay !== 'function'
    ) {
      jumpToRecipe();
      return;
    }

    const textConfig = {
      header: 'Straight to the Good Stuff! 🍎',
      body: [
        'Watch a quick ad, then we’ll jump you right to the recipe!'
      ],
      accept: 'Watch & Jump to Recipe',
      cancel: 'Keep reading'
    };

    const behaviorConfig = {
      rewardOnNoFill: true,
      rewardName: 'Jump to Recipe',
      alwaysCallback: true,
      lockScroll: true // optional: prevent page scrolling while overlay is active
    };

    window.ezRewardedAds.requestWithOverlay(
      function (result) {
        // result.reward === true means:
        // - user accepted AND finished
        // - or we no-filled but we're allowed to reward anyway
        if (result && result.reward) {
          jumpToRecipe();
        } else {
          // User declined or bailed. Do nothing.
          console.warn('Reward not granted:', result && result.msg);
        }
      },
      textConfig,
      behaviorConfig
    );
  }

  // Intercept EVERY click on links that point to "#recipe"
  document.querySelectorAll('a[href="#recipe"]').forEach(function (link) {
    link.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
      // Kill native anchor behavior hard
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      if (typeof e.stopImmediatePropagation === 'function') {
        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
      }

      // Important: do NOT mutate the hash here.
      // We only scroll & set hash AFTER reward.

      showRewardedThenMaybeJump();
    });
  });

  // EXTRA HARDENING:
  // Some themes listen for hashchange and auto-scroll.
  // If some other script tries to set location.hash = "#recipe"
  // before we've rewarded, you'll still get early scroll.
  //
  // We can guard this by temporarily "arming" a flag when the user clicks
  // the recipe link, and ignoring hashchange until we’re allowed.
  // (This is defensive; you might not need it, but it's nice insurance.)

  let allowRecipeScroll = false;

  function armBlocker() {
    allowRecipeScroll = false;
  }

  function allowScrollNow() {
    allowRecipeScroll = true;
  }

  // Patch jumpToRecipe to allow scroll afterward:
  const originalJumpToRecipe = jumpToRecipe;
  jumpToRecipe = function () {
    allowScrollNow();
    originalJumpToRecipe();
  };

  window.addEventListener('hashchange', function (evt) {
    if (
      window.location.hash === '#recipe' &&
      allowRecipeScroll === false
    ) {
      // Block premature scroll attempts driven by other code
      // by immediately undoing the hash.
      if (history.replaceState) {
        history.replaceState(null, '', ' ');
      } else {
        window.location.hash = '';
      }
    }
  });

  // When user initially clicks, arm blocker so other code can't force-scroll:
  document.querySelectorAll('a[href="#recipe"]').forEach(function (link) {
    link.addEventListener('click', armBlocker, { capture: true });
  });

});</script>
